NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
BAY OF BENGAL GATEWAY TERMINAL PRIVATE LIMITED
Reg. Off: No. 153/82, 4th Level, Santhome High Road, M.R.C. Nagar, Raja Annamalaipuram, Chennai-600 028,
Tamil Nadu, India
Notice is hereby given that pursuant to Section 485(1) of the Companies Act, 1956, for general information that the
members of the Bay of Bengal Gateway Terminal Private Limited at the Extra-ordinary General Meeting of the Company held
on 9th day of December, 2014 at C-1, 2nd Floor, Atur House, 87A Annie Besant Road, Worli, Mumbai-400 018, have
unanimously passed the following Special Resolution to wind up the above Company voluntarily:
“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the consent of the
members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as the members’ voluntary
winding up.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 490(1)(a) of the Companies Act, 1956, Mr. Pramod
S. Shah and Mr. B. Amarnadh Company Secretary in Whole Time Practice are appointed as the Joint Liquidators of the
Company for the purpose of the members’ voluntary winding up of the affairs of the Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT the consent of the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to sanction the
remuneration of liquidator of INR 2,35,000/- (Rupees Two Lakhs Thirty Five Thousand Only), plus applicable service tax,
for the winding up of the affairs of the Company.

330

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

[Part VI—Sec. 4

RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Mr. Pramod S. Shah and Mr. B. Amarnadh, the joint liquidators be and is hereby authorized
to exercise such powers as per the provisions of the Companies Act, 1956 for effectively winding up the affairs of the
Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT notwithstanding the appointment of joint liquidators the Board of Directors of the Company
be and is hereby authorized to exercise such powers in connection with the liquidation of the Company like filing of statement
of affairs with the liquidator, filing of return with the Registrar of Companies as and when required, and such other matters
incidental to the liquidation of the Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Mr. Pramod S. Shah and Mr. B. Amarnadh the, Joint Liquidators appointed by the
Company, inter alia, be and is hereby empowered to exercise the following powers:
*

To institute or defend any suit, prosecution or other legal proceedings, civil or criminal in the name of and on behalf
of the company;

*

To carry on the business of the company so far as may be necessary for the beneficial winding of the company;

*

To sell the immovable and movable property and actionable claims of the Company by public auction or private
contract, with power to transfer the whole thereof to any person or body corporate, or to sell the same in parcels;

*

To raise on the security of the assets of the company any money requisite;

*

To engage the services of professional consultants and generally defray all costs and expenses including the
professional charges;

*

To do all such other things as may be necessary for winding up the affairs of the company and distributing its assets.

Chennai
29th January 2015.

for Bay of Bengal Gateway Terminal Private Limited.
(B. AMARNADH)
Liguidator,
Director.

I, G. Seetharaman, Biological son of Thiru N. Gurumurthy, born on 5th May 1971 residing at Old No. 19, New No. 13,
Venkateswara Street, Radha Nagar, Chrompet, Chennai-600 044, by a way of this public notice inform that (late)
Thiru K. Rajamani Sasthrigal, has legally adopted me as his son on 1st day of February 1985 by a way of registered deed
bearing No. 48/1985 on the Registrar Office, Chennai Central, Chennai-600 018, My adopted Father (late) Thiru K. Rajamani
Sasthrigal Passed away on 16th June 1987. Here after I shall be known as R. Sridharan.
Chennai,

G. SEETHARAMAN.

29th January 2015.
